Free Talk

"Civilization Lamp for Women"

—Han Feng

Late Qing dynasty storytelling novel, recently obtained a book called Illustrated 20th Century Civilization Lamp for Women, by Zhong Qingxin Qing, revised by the owner of Pingquan Pavilion, published by Mingming Xue She in June of the Xuantong third year, a lithographed horizontal book, probably a reading material sold at roadside stalls. The book includes a preface by the owner of Pingquan Pavilion. The preface said of the storytelling:

"In today's society, people of all kinds are competing for storytelling novels. In Shanghai alone, there are no less than hundreds of places. And storytelling is especially trusted by women, often their shoes and socks intertwined, laughing and talking related. And the storyteller sitting in the corner sings the opening, then no one is translating. Once completed, mouth-speaking gestures, with relish to the book, but three smile marriage, falling gold fan and other adultery matters, and beautify its name talented scholars and beautiful women, so that listeners are dizzy, spread as good talk, turn to imitate, this is why society is decadent. Therefore, improving Liang Xu Jianyi Si, no less than compiling a female school textbook."

The wide influence of storytelling, the numerous book fields, the bad effect of selling storytelling, and the necessity of improvement are all evident here. The author in the book also discussed the old storytelling being unsuitable for the present day, and the benefits of this revised "Civilization Lamp for Women":

Female education has been in decline for a thousand years, textbooks should be in seven-character verses. Wonderful, teach loyalty, filial piety and chastity, but some are excessive, and he has not escaped a few chapters of his study. The remaining customs of Ren and Si have not died out, this tune can be counted as Lu Lingguang. Only worry about evil consequences repeatedly, talented scholars and beauties spread matters. Fruit report, depicting picking orchids and cheating with concubines; Shuangzhufeng, promoting stealing jade and stealing fragrance; Sun Shenghua, one husband and many wives ruin ethics; Rebirth fate, women dressing as men disrupt discipline. That's it, the seven characters build an equal boundary, a sound wakes up the silk incense. Adding hundreds of millions to complete personality, not counting three thousand powder Dai lines.

The author is very proud of this story, so the dialogue also includes: "Specially wrote the Civilization Lamp story for women, designed to improve the women's society. Relying on the Dharma drum and conch, making people wake up: or can salvage the overall situation, reverse the universe." "Civilization is piled up, the tune is sonorous, most suitable for boudoir daughter's intestines." However, although it can not be as the author said, has that kind of influence, but his spirit of opening up new territory is valuable. Because in storytelling novels, old works, with very few exceptions, are always unable to jump out of the "talented scholar and beautiful woman", "heroic sons and daughters" two types, and the author can have such a vision, is always difficult.

The book has eight acts: Education, Unbound Feet, Arts, Superstition, Child Brides, Breaking Prison, Tea Party, Rejection of Treaty. Using Ms. Beauty-Pi's spirit of tea to the East, visiting Confucius' mother in Qufu, transporting the civilization of Europe and the West to open the scene. The content of each scene can be seen in the synopsis. It should be added that "Breaking Prison" is about rescuing child brides from dark families, "Rejecting Treaty" is about the Chinese Exclusion Act in the United States, and the anti-foreign goods movement in China, and "Tea Party" is about free gatherings of men and women to open up the atmosphere. The first scene, the opening:

Explain the national responsibility, to fulfill the freedom of duty. Do not say it is the skirt

Hairpin, men and women out equal. Equal equality, idle reading Rousseau's political theory (Dan quoted, like a dream order)

This can explain a trend in the writing world at that time, that is, to try to use new nouns, new terms, to show the depth of their new learning. The novel "New Karma Mirror" once satirized this tendency very fiercely, saying that a new scholar recorded new nouns into a secret book, and after the manuscript was written, he took out the useful ones from the secret book and embedded them one by one, replacing the old terms in the original manuscript. This is certainly excessive, but the prevalence of the tendency is visible. Although "Civilization Lamp" also uses new nouns, most of it is very natural. The other exceptions, such as "Husband is talented, knows the words of Brahma; family is quiet, idle to turn Rousseau's book one", but not much. Among all the books, the lyrics in "Reject Treaty" are the most readable:

A wooden house is imprisoned with new entry, the dream soul is tragically broken in the old hometown. Thinking of who lost the power of the early development of the Americas, cutting thorns and removing thorns is our yellow species. To this day, the land is wide open and the sweat is forgotten, and we treat our compatriots like half sheep. Thinking about it, they are all guests from other continents, but other kinds are not as strong as white. As long as Japan can be self-reliant recently, it will meet everywhere and be widely praised. This time, the harsh treaty is revised, do not say that our people are easy to show strength. Fortunately, the gentry and merchants are seeking to boycott, not selling American goods and rejecting the ocean.

Regarding literary works about the "Chinese Exclusion Act", I have seen a chapter in Liang Qichao's "Travel Notes of the New World" (New People's Cong Bao temporary supplement), novels such as "New Story of Rejecting Treaty", "Bitter Society", etc., and this is the first kind in storytelling. The effectiveness of such writing, without doubt, is greater than that of works that are pedantic. The content of "Civilization Lamp", is indeed as the author said, is a textbook, introducing new knowledge of female innovation.

The eight acts I have seen are the upper volume, and it is not possible to verify whether the lower volume has been published, because most of the books were published in installments at that time, and very few were printed at the same time. But even this can glimpse the whole. This book is now more rare than "Gengzi National Change Storytelling", "National Change Storytelling" is made by the hands of learned people, and is thread-bound, and there are still people collecting it. I am afraid that there are no collectors of this kind of door-panel book. There is an illustration in each act, some of which are good.

Appendix: The previous work "Another Boxer Storytelling" one meaning, after getting "National Change Storytelling", began to know that the former is the first twenty chapters of reading, is a falsely printed edition, in fact, not two books, I hope readers pay attention.

The Weariness of Life

—Already

Bearing the burden of life, I have walked nearly ten years of my life journey with great hardship, and now I feel exhausted and unable to continue to catch up with this unfinished journey!

Is the path of the world flat or rugged? Perhaps it is flat? I see some people walking easily and comfortably, without any sign of pain. Even myself, in the decades before ten years ago, when I was being led by others and the burden of life was not yet pressed down on my shoulders, wasn't I also walking a flat path in the world? However, it is clearly rugged. The past ten years, I, and the group who share the same fate with me, have tasted the infinite bitterness of this rugged path of the world. It goes without saying that we have been subjected to the attacks of wind, frost, rain, and dew. At what moment have our feet not been pricked and bleeding by the thorns on the road!

I think it was because I was young and strong at that time, or because the burden of life was lighter. In the first few years of setting out on the journey, my spirit was excited, my mood was happy, my spirit was brave, my will was strong, and my hope was bright. On the road, no matter how much pain I suffered or how many obstacles I encountered, they could not make my advancing footsteps shrink back in fear of difficulty. But how is it now?

Now, on this journey of life, I feel extremely tired! I also know that the journey of life only has a path to go, and there is no way back. We should strive to move forward, that is the solution. To retreat is to perish. But to move forward, I am really too tired! I no longer have the strength to carry the burden that is getting heavier on my shoulders. I have suffered enough of the grinding of body and mind. Even if I want to struggle again, it is a bit difficult. I admit that I am cowardly! I have to temporarily stop my feet and take a breath beside this halfway. But is it possible for me to do this?

I stretch my neck and look forward. The distance of the journey is unknown. It is separated by mountains and rivers, clouds and fog, overlapping and vast. But oh, even if this is a journey that cannot be reached, is overlapping, and is vast, I cannot but reluctantly rally my dissipated energy and take on this burden of life. Panting, dripping with sweat, walking forward step by step with great difficulty, to the end of this journey of life, when I am still alive. I really don't dare to look back at the hideous and terrifying face of the demon of life that is whipping me from behind!

— Fan Hai

My hatred for you,

Hatred beyond the hatred of killing my father!

In the sky,

There are no two suns;

On the ground,

Mourning (Part 1)

— Pillow Stone

I should replace all the words of mourning with crying. However, when I learned of your death, I did not cry either. I just remained silent, silent. In this silence, great hidden pain played out in my heart. I myself also find it strange that after years of cruel torment, I have completely lost the ability to cry. For me, there is only hatred. You know, hatred gnaws at my heart, and the pain is even more unbearable than crying!

At this time last year, our mother was entangled by illness and died. At that time, I could hardly cry out tears or sounds, only the past events of my mother suffering for her children repeatedly, endlessly涌上心頭, like a sharp drill, piercing my heart, piercing every piece of flesh on my body. In the moment when my mother died, when she纹痛得大聲嘶喊到沒有了聲音也沒有了氣息的时分, our old father was crying, our siblings were crying, my wife was crying, even my young son was crying in his dream. But oh! Second brother, you do not know the tragic state of our mother's death at that time, although she did not forget you, who had no news for years, on the day before her death, but now, I know that you have died a year before our mother.

When the setting sun is on the barren grass, and crows are flying and crowing in the tile rubble field, where the tombs are scattered, where can I find your bones? Moreover, the invisible fences block my return journey. How can I go to your grave to worship? Oh! Infinite hatred in the world, where to cry for the lonely soul? Second brother! I should only look up to the sky and let the tears flow far to my heart! Forever, forever, it is desolate and hateful,

The torment of the past few years has made me an incomplete person who has lost his emotions, but deep impressions can still evoke my memories. I remember it was an evening on the Mid-Autumn Festival. I began to flee, and began to drift to the ends of the earth to be a wandering person.

Stealing Taro

— Li Sanlang

The black night, the southern countryside is vastly unfolded like a large and dark curtain, and the sparse villages are quietly submerged in the night, the trees rustle like huge demons, the terrible sounds of mourning and the women's tearful sobs. The uneven hills can still be vaguely captured by people's eyes, and the rice stalks in the paddy fields sway gently with the weeds by the roadside.

People are like in a dream, and only the busy dogs can be heard barking in the distance.

There is no moon, the sky is full of sorrow. A few small stars that are still struggling emit a kind of crying light.

A-Qian's wife quietly carries a dustpan and a hoe, and runs lightly on the familiar mountain path overgrown with weeds. On tiptoe, for fear of being seen by others. Although in that dark and calm mountain field, she does not worry about being devoured by ghosts or beasts, she is most afraid of meeting someone in the green forest. ——Alas, stealing taro, a thief of stealing taro. If she gets caught, she will not only be fined ten yuan but also be humiliated! However, it is not afraid of being humiliated. There are enough people stealing things these days. Like that rich second aunt, she even hired many people to cultivate the land. Stealing from other people's homes is unconscionable, bah! Who says it is not right to steal from her home? However, in case, where to get ten yuan? There is basically nothing to eat, and her husband is sick, so she does this.

Thinking, running, her heart jumping uneasily. ——A load also gets three or five yuan...

The field is dead, there is no turbulent sound, only the wind, only the wind that sweeps the hearts of the people, like sharp arrows, piercing her tense heart one by one. Her tired and hungry eyes, which were sunk, emitted light in the dark night.

On one high taro field after another, she was busy turning over the loose soil with her hands and feet. Following that, one by one, like field rats, hairy taro rolled out, round, long, small, in pairs, swaying her heart like gold; yes, she had never smiled so excitedly, in the dark night, she could vaguely reveal the smile marks on her long face.

There was no sound on the earth, she was afraid that her hoe would disturb the male watchman who was watching over another mountain forest. ——Immediately, several blurred, terrible blood-like faces released a sneer, and several guns aimed at her as if drawing, thick ropes, and the second aunt's fat mouth, always endlessly,啧啧 ground cursing, rotten smelly goods, old 　　(Note: that is, prostitute), that strange ugly look, snake-like sounds constantly pouring out of her head. Wasn't A-Si's wife dragged into the group security bureau like that half a month ago? ——Hey! How terrible it is.

She calmed her mind and quickly loaded it into the dustpan. She could not feel the weight of the thirty or forty pounds of fresh taro on her shoulders, but she felt as if some hateful guy was dragging behind the burden. The more she was afraid of being caught up, the more desperately her two legs had to run, panting, and the person seemed to be swaying like a torrent. Only when she carried the load to her own toilet pit, did she feel at ease, and she hurriedly buried the taro in a large pile of ash that she picked out from her home every day, dropped the load, and pretended to be normal and walked away as if she had returned from urinating in the toilet pit.

The next morning, the village spread the news that someone had stolen the second aunt's taro. The fat woman cursed as if she had lost gold:

"The one who stole my taro will be struck by lightning, either dead or a rotten smelly thing, you! Eating my taro will definitely be unlucky..."

Never mind her, A-Qian's wife smiled secretly, and also planned how to pick it to the market to sell it.

Three Days (5)

— Luo Hong

Huang Zhongpu revealed his upper row of yellowed teeth again, and the six or seven wrinkles on his forehead were squeezed tightly together, his face looking pitiful as if he were afraid of being beaten. It was as if, whether Youfa or Youcai had any ideas, Master Lu would respond to them respectfully with a single word. He understood Master Lu's temper best; if others argued with him, he would never let it go easily. If Youfa and the others didn't agree to this condition, Master Lu would get angry and not only refuse to lend money, but might also resort to other means, such as...

Huang Zhongpu was truly like a roundworm in Master Lu's stomach. Sure enough, Master Lu stood up, flicked away the two-fen-long cigarette butt, and said to him in a low voice:

"Is today the seventeenth?"

"Yesterday was the twenty-sixth - that's right, today is the twenty-seventh."

"In that case, the two hundred yuan they borrowed from the Longhui will be due in only three days. Hmph, who dares to delay payment to the Longhui by even half a day? They'll have to find a way. I say, Zhongpu—"

Master Lu took another step closer to Huang Zhongpu, looking strangely intimate. "Go tell the local constable to press Youfa's family a little harder. Let's see how tough they can be!"

Huang Zhongpu agreed repeatedly. He had a greasy feeling in his heart. Whenever Master Lu showed him some intimacy, he felt a strange greasiness in his heart, as if he were being stroked by a woman's hand. He had been Master Lu's confidant, relying on Master Lu to supplement him with fifty or sixty yuan each year, for over twenty years now, but he had only had that greasy feeling three times. Once was during the locust plague, when the Longhui was being formed. Magistrate Wang and the others wanted to store the grain in the township office, as a place to accumulate grain. Master Lu was terribly anxious and wanted Huang Zhongpu to come up with an idea. He came up with the suggestion to have the local constables tell Magistrate Wang and the others that storing the grain in the township office was unreliable because the township office was noisy, and if something went wrong, no one would take responsibility. Master Lu's family had spacious granaries, and dividing out two rooms would be enough, and Master Lu had always been enthusiastic about public welfare, and he would certainly not begrudge those two rooms and refuse to lend them out. After saying this several times, the matter was successfully resolved. At that time, Master Lu had praised him for being capable and praised him very intimately. The second time was last year when Master Lu celebrated his fiftieth birthday but didn't have a son. He had married three concubines, but they had only given birth to daughters. Master Lu valued the "lack of descendants being the greatest act of unfilial piety," so he was very worried about this matter. Huang Zhongpu understood his concerns and acted as a matchmaker. He had often heard Master Lu say that Zhou Si's daughter was very beautiful, and if she were dressed better, she would be more beautiful than his three concubines. So he repeatedly discussed it with Zhou Si, and the engagement that had been promised for one hundred yuan was canceled. Zhou Si's daughter, with her melon-seed face, became Master Lu's fourth concubine. It could also be said that this young girl was fortunate enough to give birth to a son. So, on the day of the full moon celebration, Master Lu had intimately toasted him a cup of wine. Now, this time was considered the third time.

"Only three days left. Don't worry, Master, they can't escape. Without you, Master, they wouldn't be able to borrow money. It's no use if that kid Youcai is stubborn. The Longhui's money must be repaid when it's due. I'm not afraid of him stopping his wife from being a wet nurse!" He also imitated Master Lu's way of speaking, as if reciting an article, drawing out each word.

"Mmm... mmm," Master Lu hummed in his throat, with his hands tucked into his sleeves, pacing back and forth with his head lowered. Seeing this, Huang Zhongpu knew that he didn't need to say anything more to him; Master Lu had already thought of something. So Huang Zhongpu bid farewell and walked out.

Brief Comments

Taiyuan Prostitutes Implement Perming Hair and Wearing High Heels

— Meng Ruo

Everyone knows that Shanxi Province is a place with a very pure social atmosphere. However, now I hear that prostitutes in Taiyuan are all going to perm their hair and wear high heels, which is a bit unusual.

Prostitutes perming their hair and wearing high heels is not uncommon in itself. What's strange is that the implementation of perming hair and wearing high heels by prostitutes in Taiyuan is not the prostitutes' own desire, but rather they are being forced to do so.

But don't mistakenly think that the social atmosphere in Shanxi Province is about to change. It should be known that the current perming of hair and wearing high heels by prostitutes in Taiyuan is not intentionally trying to become extravagant, but rather to make the originally pure social atmosphere even purer.

Originally, the intention behind requiring all prostitutes in Taiyuan to perm their hair and wear high heels was to "distinguish them from respectable women."

Perming hair and wearing high heels is a modern style of dress. I have never been to Shanxi Province or Taiyuan. I'm not sure if there are modern women in Taiyuan, and whether the modern women there also perm their hair and wear high heels. But judging from the phrase "distinguish them from respectable women," even the modern women in Taiyuan, presumably, do not perm their hair and wear high heels. Therefore, some people, in order to make the pure social atmosphere in Shanxi Province even purer, have ordered prostitutes to perm their hair and wear high heels to avoid the risk of confusing the genuine with the fake.

Naturally, prostitutes are not respectable women, but rather non-respectable women. Since prostitutes are non-respectable women, their attire naturally cannot be the same as that of respectable women. In that case, the implementation of all prostitutes in Taiyuan perming their hair and wearing high heels is very meaningful. Moreover, in addition to perming hair and wearing high heels, they must also wear a "peach blossom badge." This also symbolizes that they are a kind of wild grass and idle flowers.

However, some people say that asking prostitutes to perm their hair and wear high heels only benefits the prostitutes and does no harm. Because what prostitutes sell is their bodies, their attire must be fashionable in order to attract customers. Now that all the prostitutes in Taiyuan are perming their hair and wearing high heels, this will undoubtedly have some effect in attracting a bunch of lecherous men.

However, my view is different from this. Now, women in Taiyuan are probably gradually becoming fashionable, and there are also those who perm their hair and wear high-heeled leather shoes. Therefore, the authorities have ordered prostitutes to perm their hair and wear high-heeled leather shoes, so that respectable women dare not perm their hair or wear high-heeled leather shoes again. If a respectable woman wears high-heeled leather shoes and perms her hair again, she will be considered a prostitute. This is an excellent method of prohibiting extravagance. However, truly fashionable respectable women are not afraid of being suspected of being prostitutes and will not stop wearing high-heeled leather shoes and perming their hair.

Night Berth

— Ye Fei

The boat had just passed the Yellow Crane Gate when it started to rain; and according to the boatman, there would probably be a big storm tonight, wouldn't we suffer another misfortune! Everyone's heart felt like it was weighed down by dozens of pounds of lead, and it kept sinking, sinking; looking at the sky, it was gradually darkening. If we continued to move forward in this storm, not only would we still not reach our destination today, but there might be many dangers ahead: even as it is, letting it carry more than twenty people and floating on this white-crested tide is really worrying.

A not-very-large boat was floating on a huge lake, like a leaf carrying dozens of ants floating in the river; with just one jolt, there was a risk of capsizing. Under these circumstances, everyone's face seemed to be covered with a layer of fear. But even if we were anxious, it was useless. Besides trying our best to calm our restless hearts and comforting ourselves, we could only entrust our entire lives to this civilian boat.

Now everyone's only hope was that the sky would clear up immediately. If it didn't rain and there was no wind, then even sailing at night would be fine.

"Boatman, what should we do? We're adrift in the middle of the lake in this wind and

Page 18

rain, and we're cold and hungry. Let's find a small port to dock in!" Everyone unanimously urged the boatman.

"This is the weather; what can I do? Don't worry, let's get into Xiangshan Port first," the boatman said, leaning one hand on the tiller and puffing on his pipe, comforting everyone gently.

"How far is it from here to Xiangshan Port?" This was a woman's voice.

"It's close!" he said, pointing with a dry pipe toward the bow of the boat. Sure enough, a pile of dark shadows was gradually moving toward the bow. "That mountain shadow is Xiangshan Port."

More than twenty people were huddled under the oilcloth awning. The boat was bumping through the waves like a running horse, and the raindrops hit the awning, making a clattering sound. Several of the passengers were smoking desperately to relieve this depression, and the smoke filled the awning, causing many people to cough incessantly. Three ladies, however, were vomiting over the side of the boat because they couldn't stand the rocking.

The boat slowly sailed in the rain, and the surrounding area was entirely ruled by the god of darkness; however, at this time, we couldn't find a second boat on the surrounding lake besides ours. The sound of the rain on the awning and the sound of the waves under the boat were harmoniously accompanying us, but everyone's mood in the boat was immersed in depression and restlessness. They were only staring blankly at the dim mast light. The light reflected on everyone's faces, and everyone was equally pale and listless. In every pair of eyes, however, was a light of annoyance.

At dusk, the boat finally entered Xiangshan Port and tied up under a large poplar tree, preparing to hide there for the night.

Everyone felt much relieved, but the stomachs that hadn't been filled all day couldn't help but rebel. I finally couldn't help but negotiate with the boatman, asking them to find something to fill our stomachs.

"Boatman, we haven't eaten anything all day, and we're really hungry now. Is there any way to solve this?" I asked the boatman.

"Today we have to ask the boat boss to prepare dinner for us; it's not okay to spend the night on an empty stomach. Anyway, everyone will pay for the food," the crowd echoed. But because there wasn't enough rice and there were too many people, they only cooked two pots of porridge. Everyone was extremely hungry, so even without vegetables, they could drink the plain porridge. The two pots of porridge were quickly snatched clean in no time, and several people still seemed not to have had enough.

Although our empty stomachs were finally filled, sleeping was another problem. How could the deck, which was less than ten feet long and no more than five feet wide, accommodate more than twenty people? And everyone had not brought bedding; although it was already late spring and early summer, it was still so chilly at night. So, except for a few who were snoring and sleeping soundly, most people sat slumped and hadn't closed their eyes once.

The Temptation of the Bridal Sedan Chair

— Yi An

Life is Like a Lonely Lamp

— Cheng Quan

Life is like a lonely lamp. It is just many of them strung together, or perhaps in twos and threes, floating in the boundless torrent of time, flickering, flashing, gathering and scattering. The light is faint, hazy—and sometimes, perhaps, there are one or two that glaringly emit a strong light, but in the torrent of time, in the entire universe, carefully looking, they are merely like shooting stars flashing by; following this stubborn, tragic flash is the inevitable shattering and annihilation, and what remains in this torrent of time is merely a pile of useless ashes. If one day a strong wind arises in the universe, and there are one or two or even extremely weak waves in the stream of time, then who has the courage to guarantee that those annihilated ashes will not be submerged to the bottom of the great river—to an infinitely deep bottom?

But these submerged, annihilated ashes, just a tenth of a second before, had illuminated one or two specks of dust, or even a tiny space of a thousandth of a square inch, with the faint light of life! Like a ghost in the wilderness.

(Can you really admit that this tragedy is supremely fair?)

But let us, like a botanist observing a small cotyledon, carefully look: Life, even if it is as weak as a lonely lamp in the torrent of the world, still has a moving and strong charm for the creatures that multiply on its surface! Its light is dim, but only it can be said to truly understand how to make people live patiently! It uses a faint light that can barely illuminate a grain of rice, and it always places this ghost-like light an inch in front of people, constantly boasting and enticing; thus, it makes people confusedly follow it, until they exhaust hundreds of thousands of a second of time and the faint light of life dies out at the same time, and they are submerged at the same time...!

To say that life is just a supremely weak lonely lamp, but for all of mankind, it is a supremely profound mystery. People look at it just as an astronomer uses unreliable instruments to observe distant planets; when he is amazed by many fine lines and mixed colors, he is also bewildered by an unsolvable mystery. Who has ever remembered that the dim gold at the bottom of the starlight is the laughter of a long-gone childhood; and who else dares to turn over the old shadows of green youth and purple love? Thus, what exists in this faint lonely light, the freshest and most indelible, is only the dark red trap of suffering and the dark shadow of old age.

As if endlessly, people are jumping, working, building, enduring, and displaying in different directions under the lonely lamp of life. The scenes on the road of life pass by in clusters. People pass through mountains and rivers, rolling in mud pits and climbing over thorns, but who has ever given up the power of life, who has ever forgotten the instinct to survive, and finally, who has ever carefully scrutinized a fleeting meteor in midsummer night?

Life is like a weak lonely lamp, but let us learn to praise this lonely lamp, even if it is weak, but has a strong charm; only it can make people live with more fervent goodwill; only it can place its weak light an inch in front of us, enticing and boasting. We are walking step by step, even if what awaits us in the end is a grave, ashes; even if life is a flickering fire in a thousandth of a second; let everything be! Life is a lonely lamp in the torrent of time!

Great Shanghai Will Soon Screen "Arctic Exploration Disaster Record"

"Arctic Exploration Disaster Record" is a historical treasure that records the Soviet Arctic exploration of 1934. When the exploration team set off from Russia, newspapers from various countries reported it, recognizing it as a major event in modern exploration history. The entire exploration team of one hundred and four members set off on the icebreaker "Chelyuskin", experiencing all kinds of difficulties and obstacles. Unfortunately, the "Chelyuskin" was crushed by floating ice midway, and the exploration team members escaped to the ice, drifting for two months. Finally, they were rescued by the Soviet Air Force at risk and were able to return alive.

This film was actually taken by the famous photographer Shavlovran, who accompanied the exploration team. Therefore, the entire film is a true-life scene and is a rare find among exploration films. The screening of the film has been decided to begin on the 8th at the Great Shanghai Grand Theater in this city. It is heard that along with the film, there will also be newsreels of Mei Lanfang's recent performance in Russia and the Soviet International Film Exhibition.

Xu Lai and Hu Jia Have Both Fallen

Director Shen Xiling's "Boatman's Daughter" depicts rural bankruptcy and social economic panic, causing those kind souls to eventually become bad people under the pressure of a poor environment. Xu Lai and Hu Jia, these two true country girls, were abducted to the city and sold to a brothel, forcing them to become prostitutes. When those drunken customers raised their glasses full of wine and smiled vaguely, "Girl! Drink a glass for Grandpa's sake!" Although they were already drunk, they had to smile bitterly, take the glass, and drink wildly.

When filming this scene, Shen Xiling, with a mournful face, asked others for advice everywhere, saying that his own experience was insufficient.

Shen Bao Local Supplement - Automobile Weekly

New Trends in American Heavy and Light Cars

— Zhenmin

In recent years, the biggest change in the American automobile market has been the rise of light cars and the decline of heavy cars. Previously, the sales of heavy cars accounted for almost 80% of the total number of cars. The main reason for this popularity was probably that engineers designed heavy cars with particular precision. The bodies of heavy cars were extremely sturdy and streamlined, and their interiors were very luxurious. In contrast, light cars at that time were truly inferior.

Indeed, the design of heavy cars, due to their large mass, made the problem of center of gravity distribution relatively easy to solve. With a little attention during planning, an appropriate weight and volume ratio could be achieved, making the car very stable during driving, without any impact whatsoever.

However, the situation was different for light cars. The distribution of the center of gravity was most difficult. Often, a light car would be well-designed, but when actually driven, it would be prone to overturning under strong acceleration. In the past, in American long-distance racing, many drivers lost their lives due to light car rollovers. These past failures of light cars are truly worthy of study.

After various failures, engineers have gradually discovered the crux of the matter. New light cars now have their center of gravity lowered as much as possible, and the body is also lowered, with the pedals close to the ground. This is the greatest success in the practical design of light cars in recent years.

In recent years, the problem of space has become increasingly serious in cities around the world due to population growth. Large heavy cars, driving on busy roads, not only take up a lot of space, but are also difficult to maneuver. This is the main reason for the rise of light cars in recent years.

In general, car owners are very satisfied with the economic benefits of using light cars. First, light cars are flexible in operation. Second, daily inspections are simple and convenient. Third, in the event of a breakdown, light cars can be quickly repaired and restored to their original condition. All of this has left a deep impression on car owners.

Last year, Ford's 8 to 10 horsepower light car sales reached 68%. The completeness of this light car's construction is truly admirable. The roof is now made of all steel, and it is extremely streamlined, which was rare in the past for light cars. Furthermore, there are five steps for changing speeds, rapid braking, and agile acceleration gear action, especially.

Morris's best-selling light car last year was also astounding. Heavy cars only accounted for 30% of sales. The sale of the Hillman Minx has been popular for a while. According to users, the average gasoline and repair costs per mile when using a light car are 25% less than when using a heavy car. In ordinary engineering practice, the larger the engine, the less power is lost. Now, the small engine of a light car is economical. This is indeed the strangest question.

Currently, most of the cars on the streets of American cities are between 10 and 15 horsepower. The next most common are 15 to 20 horsepower. The fewest are vehicles with 25 horsepower or more. Cars traveling on highways are almost entirely light cars with 10 to 20 horsepower. This new trend has never been seen before.

In the past, another reason why car owners did not trust light cars was their low speed. Because light cars have small engines, limited cylinder volume, and a small compression ratio, the engine's power is reduced, and a high speed cannot be achieved. But this is no longer a problem. Although the engine is small, the compression ratio has been greatly increased, and with the addition of well-matched gears, the speed has increased significantly. Now, let's list the increase in light car speeds in recent years as follows:

Year Horsepower Top Speed (Miles per Hour)

1929 10 hp 50

1930 10 hp 80

1931 10 hp 90

1932 10 hp 95

1933 10 hp 105

1934 10 hp 150

1935 10 hp 200

From the above table, it can be seen that the speed of light cars has been increasing in recent years. Because of the high speed, the structure of the cylinders has also been greatly improved. The metal of the cylinders is now made of a special alloy, which is hard and resistant to acid. The excellence of the radiator is unmatched by ordinary heavy cars.

The craze for light car manufacturing among American car factories this year is almost unquestionable. Given the current situation, although heavy cars have not been completely abandoned by light cars, the future automobile market will undoubtedly belong entirely to light cars.

The New Oldsmobile

— Fu

—Knee-Action Wheels and Other Features—

The Knee-Action wheel is the greatest contribution to driving comfort in the history of automobiles. This is proven by the experience of millions of car owners over the years. Oldsmobile engineers, having verified the effectiveness of Knee-Action through millions of Oldsmobile cars in 1934, decided to continue to apply it to every Oldsmobile produced in 1935, making it a standard feature without increasing the price.

When considering why Oldsmobile has become more comfortable with the application of Knee-Action, it is because its front wheels can move up and down independently without being constrained by each other. The bumps and vibrations that used to be transmitted through the front axle to all other parts of the car are now eliminated by Knee-Action. When driving over ruts or encountering bumps, the coil springs of the front wheels can absorb the vibrations without transmitting them to the car or the passengers. Furthermore, the alignment of the wheels is also more precise, which extends the life of the tires.

What is particularly noteworthy is that Knee-Action also greatly enhances safety. The use of these front wheels makes central management steering possible, making handling natural and easy in critical situations. For added safety, the 1935 Oldsmobile also features improved self-energizing hydraulic brakes with increased braking area of 14%. The action is sensitive, precise, and extremely easy to operate.

Another advantage of the Oldsmobile six-cylinder and eight-cylinder models is sound insulation. The car's chassis and engine are completely soundproofed using scientifically sound principles. The Fisher all-steel solid top and door panels are made of excellent insulation material to prevent noise from entering. In addition, features such as a completely silent helical gear transmission, three-point rubber-mounted engine brackets, and specially designed mufflers are all found in the Oldsmobile. This is why it is the only quiet and beautiful car.

Another Batch of New LaFayette Cars on Display

— Yun

Another batch of new LaFayette cars produced by Nash Motors has arrived in Shanghai. The local dealer, Hejin Company, will display them in the showroom at the end of this week for public viewing. These new cars are priced in the lowest category, but their seven-bearing crankshaft, 18-horsepower engine, and 39 other fine features are unique to LaFayette. Other low-priced vehicles certainly do not have them all. Mr. Greenblatt, the sales manager of Hejin, told people that these new cars truly offer all the advantages of a Nash engine to new car owners. At such a low price, it would have been difficult to manufacture such a perfect car in the past. Today, due to advancements in the factory's production methods, favorable raw material market transactions, and various other factors, this unprecedented masterpiece can be achieved. The new car's engine uses a five-point rubber mount, so its operation is silent and does not cause vibrations. Full pressure lubrication, with pressurized oil supplied to the piston pins and cylinder walls, are all features of large cars, which are now found in cars at such a low price. The new car is 189.5 inches long overall, extremely spacious and comfortable. The four-door sedan has an interior length of 86 inches from the partition to the rear window. Another feature of the new car is its new ventilation system. Regardless of the weather, one can enjoy extremely quiet ventilation without obstructing the passenger's view or being exposed to gusts of wind. With so many advantages at such a low price, these new cars will undoubtedly be warmly welcomed by the general public once they are released. This can be stated with certainty.

A Collection of Automobile News

— Yu

The Relationship Between Cars and Women: Lord Nuffield of England recently gave a speech at Oxford, praising women's driving. He did not admit that they were a threat. They are really no different from male drivers. Nuffield said, "If you think that there are many neurotic women drivers, I can agree. But if you say that they are all bad, then I completely disagree." Lord Nuffield continued, people who use cars should express their gratitude to women in many ways, because they have greatly helped the current development of cars. This has always been overlooked. All car colors, interior decoration, parts, ease of driving, and body styles, it can be said that none of them are not influenced by them. Regarding the activity of the British Morris Motor factory, Nuffield also mentioned that the time when Morris production reaches one car per minute is not far away.

Increased German Automobile Production: In 1934, Germany manufactured a total of 130,000 cars. This number increased by 58% compared to 1933. However, it has not reached the amount hoped for by the government. Since the abolition of horsepower tax, German automobile production in 1933 has doubled. However, last year's autumn seasonal demand declined, which was unprecedented. Although production did not increase sufficiently, public demand continued to advance. This can be seen from two points: First, the domestic production in 1934 increased by 58% compared to the previous year; Second, the sales of foreign cars in Germany increased to 73%. As for the reason for the decline in German automobile production, the biggest reason is the lack of raw materials.

Continued Increase in American Car Production: In February 1934, the average weekly automobile production in the United States reached 65,000 vehicles. This year's February output has exceeded 80,000 vehicles per week. Therefore, it is estimated that the production of American cars and trucks in the first three months of this year will exceed 1,000,000 vehicles. A year ago, the automobile production in the first three months was 750,000 vehicles. Since 1930, the automobile production in the first quarter of each year has been increasing slowly but constantly. The increase in automobile production in the first quarter of 1934 is even more evident when compared with the same period in 1933. Because in the first quarter of 1933, the total production of all brands of cars was only 368,265 vehicles. Regarding the future prospects of the automobile industry, we can measure it by the resumption of activity of three companies out of the five major companies—Studebaker, Pierce-Arrow, and Willys-Overland. These three major factories were once stagnant due to the impact of the recession. Among them, the reorganization plan of Studebaker has been approved by the court. The other two are also in the process of deliberation. The increase in future production can be predicted.

On the Heat Supply of the Carburetor System (Continued)

— Lu

For modern, high-quality cars, the standard method for ensuring complete gasoline vaporization is to heat the mixture of gasoline and air before it enters the cylinder by bringing it into contact with a surface heated by the exhaust. If the air entering the carburetor itself is slowly passed around a surface heated by the exhaust to warm it, then the gasoline will naturally vaporize more easily. In this case, in practice, the heated surface is on the outside of the exhaust pipe. In addition, there is another method, which is to install an air jacket on the carburetor float bowl cover and allow a portion of the hot exhaust gas from the cylinder to pass through this air jacket to heat the gasoline inside the float bowl. The above-mentioned methods of using exhaust to heat are a great improvement over using a water jacket and cooling system water to heat, because with this type of method, the heat supplied is very high. However, to achieve the best results for gasoline vaporization, the following methods must be used to make up for deficiencies: Use an exhaust jacketed intake manifold, or a heated intake manifold, or a combined exhaust and intake manifold. In short, if you want to use ordinary commercial gasoline more economically, today's carburetors must be equipped with heating equipment (this equipment specifically refers to heating manifolds).

Many old cars, when manufactured, had satisfactory carburetor system operation because the gasoline quality was good at that time. However, now, the gasoline economy and engine operation—especially before the engine is fully warmed up—have made the drivers or owners of these cars feel very dissatisfied. In many of these old cars, the carburetor system can be modernized, and it does not cost much. If a ready-made combined exhaust and intake manifold can be purchased on the market, it can simply be replaced. Alternatively, the original intake manifold can be fitted with an exhaust jacket, which yields the same effect. Another method is to preheat the air entering the carburetor through appropriate devices. However, there is no general rule for how to modernize the carburetor system of old cars. It must be determined according to the specific circumstances of each car. In general, there are few places to modernize the carburetor system in engines where the intake manifold is not mounted on the outside. The only thing that can be done is to install a device to heat the air entering the carburetor, or to replace it with a ready-made carburetor with a water jacket or an exhaust jacket.

We know that heating air or a mixture causes it to expand and become lighter. We also know that this heated air or mixture, compared to cold air or a mixture, is drawn into the cylinder in a much lighter weight under the same engine or throttle opening. In theory, this will weaken the pressure exerted on the piston during the explosion. However, in reality, the explosion pressure generated by the heated mixture is very slightly different from the explosion pressure generated by the unheated mixture, and it has almost no significant practical significance? Unless designing an engine for a special task, such as a racing car, consider this. Not only that, using an unheated mixture is not only fuel

Page 26

uneconomical, but also the engine's operation—perhaps with the exception of hot summer weather—is very uneven.

In the past, almost all American-made cars were equipped with a carburetor stove to heat the air entering the carburetor. This device became unnecessary only after improved manifolds were developed. The following diagram shows one such carburetor stove, and its working principle is briefly described below. (The same parts in Figures A and B are indicated by the same letters.) Surrounding the outside of exhaust pipe A is an iron cylinder B. The inner diameter of the iron cylinder must be slightly larger than the outer diameter of the exhaust pipe. The iron cylinder is supported by the cylinder feet C and does not contact the exhaust pipe, leaving a considerable gap. D is a pipe, one end connected to cylinder C and the other connected to the carburetor's air intake. When the engine is in the intake stroke, outside air enters the iron cylinder from inlet E and passes through pipe D into the carburetor. Because the cylinder surrounds the exhaust pipe, the air is warmed as it passes. This warm air enters the carburetor and causes the gasoline that has already been sprayed into a mist to evaporate more easily. In some cars, the carburetor stove is not installed separately, but is directly cast as a whole unit with the exhaust. As for the pipe connecting the carburetor stove to the carburetor air intake, it is usually made of a flexible steel pipe specially used for this purpose. Although other carburetor stoves have different forms, their working principles are all the same.

To avoid insufficient or excessive heat supply to the carburetor system from the exhaust passing through the exhaust pipe, all cars are equipped with a management mechanism. The simplest and most common is a butterfly valve. The position of this butterfly valve is in the pipe connecting the exhaust pipe and the exhaust jacket. The driver can manage it from the front panel (i.e., the dashboard) through appropriate mechanical action. This device is very common, whether it is a combined exhaust and intake manifold or a heated intake manifold.

In short, to achieve fuel economy and perfect engine operation, the need for heat supply to the carburetor system has been unequivocally affirmed. While the efforts of past automobile manufacturers have made car service more perfect, the future improvements are truly boundless. Let's wait and see.
